    24 const SAMPLE_PINESCRIPT = `//@version=5
    25 strategy("My Reversal Strategy", overlay=true)
    26 
    27 // Inputs
    28 length = input.int(14, "RSI Length")
    29 overbought = input.int(70, "Overbought Level")
    30 oversold = input.int(30, "Oversold Level")
    31 
    32 // Indicators
    33 rsi = ta.rsi(close, length)
    34 ema_fast = ta.ema(close, 20)
    35 ema_slow = ta.ema(close, 50)
    36 
    37 // Conditions
    38 longCondition = ta.crossover(rsi, oversold) and ema_fast > ema_slow
    39 shortCondition = ta.crossunder(rsi, overbought) and ema_fast < ema_slow
    40 
    41 // Entries
    42 if longCondition
    43     strategy.entry("Long", strategy.long)
    44 if shortCondition
    45     strategy.entry("Short", strategy.short)
    46 
    47 // Exits
    48 strategy.exit("TP/SL", profit=200, loss=100)`;

```
/** Extract numeric parameters from PineScript using regex patterns */
function extractParams(code: string): StrategyParams {
  const num = (pattern: RegExp, fallback: number) => {
    const m = code.match(pattern);
    return m ? parseInt(m[1], 10) : fallback;
  };

  // RSI length — e.g. input.int(14, "RSI Length") or rsi(close, 14)
  const rsi_length = num(/input\.int\s*\(\s*(\d+)\s*,\s*["']?RSI/i, 0) ||
    num(/ta\.rsi\s*\(\s*\w+\s*,\s*(\d+)\s*\)/i, 14);

  // Overbought / Oversold
  const overbought = num(/input\.int\s*\(\s*(\d+)\s*,\s*["']?overbought/i, 0) ||
    num(/overbought\s*=\s*(\d+)/i, 70);

  const oversold = num(/input\.int\s*\(\s*(\d+)\s*,\s*["']?oversold/i, 0) ||
    num(/oversold\s*=\s*(\d+)/i, 30);

  // EMA periods — collect all ta.ema(close, N) occurrences
  const emaMatches = [...code.matchAll(/ta\.ema\s*\(\s*\w+\s*,\s*(\d+)\s*\)/gi)]
    .map(m => parseInt(m[1], 10))
    .sort((a, b) => a - b);

  const ema_fast = emaMatches[0] ?? num(/ema_fast\s*=.*?(\d+)/i, 20);
  const ema_slow = emaMatches[1] ?? num(/ema_slow\s*=.*?(\d+)/i, 50);

  // Symbol from strategy() title or default
  const symbolMatch = code.match(/strategy\s*\(\s*["']([^"']+)["']/i);
  const symbolHint = code.match(/\b(BTCUSDT|ETHUSDT|SOLUSDT|BNBUSDT)\b/i);
  const symbol = symbolHint ? symbolHint[1].toUpperCase() : 'BTCUSDT';

  // Timeframe
  const tfMatch = code.match(/timeframe\s*[=:]\s*["']([^"']+)["']/i);
  const timeframe = tfMatch ? tfMatch[1] : '1h';

  const lower = code.toLowerCase();
  const has_stop_loss = lower.includes('loss=') || lower.includes('stop_loss') || lower.includes('strategy.exit');
  const has_take_profit = lower.includes('profit=') || lower.includes('take_profit');
  const hasLong = lower.includes('strategy.long');
  const hasShort = lower.includes('strategy.short');
  const trade_direction: 'long' | 'short' | 'both' = (hasLong && hasShort) ? 'both' : hasShort ? 'short' : 'long';

  return { rsi_length, overbought, oversold, ema_fast, ema_slow, symbol, timeframe, has_stop_loss, has_take_profit, trade_direction };
}
```
New String: ```
/** Extract numeric parameters from PineScript using regex patterns */
function extractParams(code: string): StrategyParams {
  const num = (pattern: RegExp, fallback: number) => {
    const m = code.match(pattern);
    return m ? parseInt(m[1], 10) : fallback;
  };

  const rsi_length = num(/input\.int\s*\(\s*(\d+)\s*,\s*["']?RSI/i, 0) ||
    num(/ta\.rsi\s*\(\s*\w+\s*,\s*(\d+)\s*\)/i, 14);

  const overbought = num(/input\.int\s*\(\s*(\d+)\s*,\s*["']?overbought/i, 0) ||
    num(/overbought\s*=\s*(\d+)/i, 70);

  const oversold = num(/input\.int\s*\(\s*(\d+)\s*,\s*["']?oversold/i, 0) ||
    num(/oversold\s*=\s*(\d+)/i, 30);

  const emaMatches = [...code.matchAll(/ta\.ema\s*\(\s*\w+\s*,\s*(\d+)\s*\)/gi)]
    .map(m => parseInt(m[1], 10))
    .sort((a, b) => a - b);

  const ema_fast = emaMatches[0] ?? num(/ema_fast\s*=.*?(\d+)/i, 20);
  const ema_slow = emaMatches[1] ?? num(/ema_slow\s*=.*?(\d+)/i, 50);

  const symbolHint = code.match(/\b(BTCUSDT|ETHUSDT|SOLUSDT|BNBUSDT)\b/i);
  const symbol = symbolHint ? symbolHint[1].toUpperCase() : 'BTCUSDT';

  const tfMatch = code.match(/timeframe\s*[=:]\s*["']([^"']+)["']/i);
  const timeframe = tfMatch ? tfMatch[1] : '1h';

  const lower = code.toLowerCase();
  const has_stop_loss = lower.includes('loss=') || lower.includes('stop_loss') || lower.includes('strategy.exit');
  const has_take_profit = lower.includes('profit=') || lower.includes('take_profit');
  const hasLong = lower.includes('strategy.long');
  const hasShort = lower.includes('strategy.short');
  const trade_direction: 'long' | 'short' | 'both' = (hasLong && hasShort) ? 'both' : hasShort ? 'short' : 'long';

  return { rsi_length, overbought, oversold, ema_fast, ema_slow, symbol, timeframe, has_stop_loss, has_take_profit, trade_direction };
}

/** Extract stop-loss and take-profit percentages from PineScript strategy.exit / input definitions */
function extractRiskPct(code: string): { stop_loss_pct: number | null; take_profit_pct: number | null; position_size_pct: number | null } {
  // strategy.exit("TP/SL", profit=200, loss=100)  → ticks, approximate as pct (1 tick ≈ 0.01%)
  const lossTickM = code.match(/loss\s*=\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i);
  const profitTickM = code.match(/profit\s*=\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i);

  // input.float(2.0, "Stop Loss %") or input(2, "SL")
  const slPctM = code.match(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:stop.?loss|sl|stop)[^"']*["']/i);
  const tpPctM = code.match(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:take.?profit|tp|target)[^"']*["']/i);

  let stop_loss_pct: number | null = null;
  let take_profit_pct: number | null = null;

  if (slPctM) stop_loss_pct = parseFloat(slPctM[1]);
  else if (lossTickM) stop_loss_pct = Math.min(+(parseFloat(lossTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 20);

  if (tpPctM) take_profit_pct = parseFloat(tpPctM[1]);
  else if (profitTickM) take_profit_pct = Math.min(+(parseFloat(profitTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50);

  // position size input if any
  const posSizeM = code.match(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:position.?size|size|qty)[^"']*["']/i);
  const position_size_pct = posSizeM ? parseFloat(posSizeM[1]) : null;

  return { stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, position_size_pct };
}
```

New String: ```
    const params = extractParams(code);
    const risk = extractRiskPct(code);
    const interpretation = buildInterpretation(code, params, risk);

    if (strategyId) {
      const supabase = createClient(
        Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL') ?? '',
        Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? ''
      );
      const update: Record<string, unknown> = { ai_interpretation: interpretation, strategy_params: params };
      if (risk.stop_loss_pct !== null) update.stop_loss_pct = risk.stop_loss_pct;
      if (risk.take_profit_pct !== null) update.take_profit_pct = risk.take_profit_pct;
      if (risk.position_size_pct !== null) update.position_size_pct = risk.position_size_pct;
      await supabase.from('strategies').update(update).eq('id', strategyId);
    }

    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ interpretation, params, risk }),
      { headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
    );
```

```
  const handleAIInterpret = (strategy: Strategy) => runAnalyze(strategy, true);

  // Sync risk form when a strategy is selected
  const handleSelectStrategy = (s: Strategy) => {
    setSelectedStrategy(s);
    setRiskForm({
      stop_loss_pct: s.stop_loss_pct != null ? String(s.stop_loss_pct) : '',
      take_profit_pct: s.take_profit_pct != null ? String(s.take_profit_pct) : '',
      position_size_pct: s.position_size_pct != null ? String(s.position_size_pct) : '',
    });
  };

  const handleSaveRisk = async () => {
    if (!selectedStrategy) return;
    setSavingRisk(true);
    const patch: Partial<Strategy> = {
      stop_loss_pct: riskForm.stop_loss_pct !== '' ? parseFloat(riskForm.stop_loss_pct) : null,
      take_profit_pct: riskForm.take_profit_pct !== '' ? parseFloat(riskForm.take_profit_pct) : null,
      position_size_pct: riskForm.position_size_pct !== '' ? parseFloat(riskForm.position_size_pct) : null,
    };
    const { error } = await updateStrategy(selectedStrategy.id, patch);
    if (error) {
      toast.error(`Failed to save risk settings: ${error}`);
    } else {
      toast.success('Risk settings saved — will override global defaults on next execution', { icon: '🛡️' });
      await load();
      const updated = await getStrategies();
      const fresh = updated.find(s => s.id === selectedStrategy.id) ?? null;
      setSelectedStrategy(fresh);
    }
    setSavingRisk(false);
  };
```

```
                          className="h-8 bg-input border-border text-sm data-mono"
                        />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    {/* Show extracted values hint if AI already found them */}
                    {(selectedStrategy.stop_loss_pct || selectedStrategy.take_profit_pct) && (
                      <p className="text-[10px] text-success flex items-center gap-1">
                        ✓ AI extracted from PineScript —
                        {selectedStrategy.stop_loss_pct ? ` SL: ${selectedStrategy.stop_loss_pct}%` : ''}
                        {selectedStrategy.take_profit_pct ? ` TP: ${selectedStrategy.take_profit_pct}%` : ''}
                        {selectedStrategy.position_size_pct ? ` Size: ${selectedStrategy.position_size_pct}%` : ''}
                      </p>
                    )}
                    <Button
                      size="sm"
                      onClick={handleSaveRisk}
                      disabled={savingRisk}
                      className="h-8 gap-1.5 w-full"
                    >
                      {savingRisk ? <Loader2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5 animate-spin" /> : <Save className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
                      Save Risk Settings
                    </Button>
                  </div>
```

</action>

symbolHint[1].toUpperCase() : \'BTCUSDT\';\n\n  const tfMatch = code.match(/timeframe\\s*[=:]\\s*["\']([^"\']+)["\']/i);\n  const timeframe = tfMatch ? tfMatch[1] : \'1h\';\n\n  const lower = code.toLowerCase();\n  const has_stop_loss = lower.includes(\'loss=\') || lower.includes(\'stop_loss\') || lower.includes(\'strategy.exit\');\n  const has_take_profit = lower.includes(\'profit=\') || lower.includes(\'take_profit\');\n  const hasLong = lower.includes(\'strategy.long\');\n  const hasShort = lower.includes(\'strategy.short\');\n  const trade_direction: \'long\' | \'short\' | \'both\' = (hasLong && hasShort) ?      8 interface StrategyParams {

    21 Deno.serve(async (req) => {
    22   if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
    23 
    24   try {
    25     const { strategyId, code } = await req.json();
    26 
    27     if (!code) {
    28       return new Response(
    29         JSON.stringify({ error: 'PineScript code is required' }),
    30         { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }

    35     const risk = extractRiskPct(code);

    39       const supabase = createClient(

    41         Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? ''
    42       );

    46       if (risk.position_size_pct !== null) update.position_size_pct = risk.position_size_pct;
    47       await supabase.from('strategies').update(update).eq('id', strategyId);

    62 /** Extract numeric parameters from PineScript using regex patterns */
    63 function extractParams(code: string): StrategyParams {
    64   const num = (pattern: RegExp, fallback: number) => {
    65     const m = code.match(pattern);
    66     return m ? parseInt(m[1], 10) : fallback;
    67   };
    68 
    69   const rsi_length = num(/input\.int\s*\(\s*(\d+)\s*,\s*["']?RSI/i, 0) ||
    70     num(/ta\.rsi\s*\(\s*\w+\s*,\s*(\d+)\s*\)/i, 14);
    71 
    72   const overbought = num(/input\.int\s*\(\s*(\d+)\s*,\s*["']?overbought/i, 0) ||
    73     num(/overbought\s*=\s*(\d+)/i, 70);
    74 
    75   const oversold = num(/input\.int\s*\(\s*(\d+)\s*,\s*["']?oversold/i, 0) ||
    76     num(/oversold\s*=\s*(\d+)/i, 30);
    77 
    78   const emaMatches = [...code.matchAll(/ta\.ema\s*\(\s*\w+\s*,\s*(\d+)\s*\)/gi)]
    79     .map(m => parseInt(m[1], 10))
    80     .sort((a, b) => a - b);
    81 
    82   const ema_fast = emaMatches[0] ?? num(/ema_fast\s*=.*?(\d+)/i, 20);
    83   const ema_slow = emaMatches[1] ?? num(/ema_slow\s*=.*?(\d+)/i, 50);
    84 
    85   const symbolHint = code.match(/\b(BTCUSDT|ETHUSDT|SOLUSDT|BNBUSDT)\b/i);
    86   const symbol = symbolHint ? symbolHint[1].toUpperCase() : 'BTCUSDT';
    87 
    88   const tfMatch = code.match(/timeframe\s*[=:]\s*["']([^"']+)["']/i);
    89   const timeframe = tfMatch ? tfMatch[1] : '1h';
    90 
    91   const lower = code.toLowerCase();
    92   const has_stop_loss = lower.includes('loss=') || lower.includes('stop_loss') || lower.includes('strategy.exit');
    93   const has_take_profit = lower.includes('profit=') || lower.includes('take_profit');
    94   const hasLong = lower.includes('strategy.long');
    95   const hasShort = lower.includes('strategy.short');
    96   const trade_direction: 'long' | 'short' | 'both' = (hasLong && hasShort) ? 'both' : hasShort ? 'short' : 'long';
    97 
    98   return { rsi_length, overbought, oversold, ema_fast, ema_slow, symbol, timeframe, has_stop_loss, has_take_profit, trade_direction };
    99 }
   100 
   101 /** Extract stop-loss and take-profit percentages from PineScript strategy.exit / input definitions */
   102 function extractRiskPct(code: string): { stop_loss_pct: number | null; take_profit_pct: number | null; position_size_pct: number | null } {
   103   // strategy.exit("TP/SL", profit=200, loss=100)  → ticks, approximate as pct (1 tick ≈ 0.01%)
   104   const lossTickM = code.match(/loss\s*=\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i);
   105   const profitTickM = code.match(/profit\s*=\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i);
   106 
   107   // input.float(2.0, "Stop Loss %") or input(2, "SL")
   108   const slPctM = code.match(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:stop.?loss|sl|stop)[^"']*["']/i);
   109   const tpPctM = code.match(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:take.?profit|tp|target)[^"']*["']/i);
   110 
   111   let stop_loss_pct: number | null = null;
   112   let take_profit_pct: number | null = null;
   113 
   114   if (slPctM) stop_loss_pct = parseFloat(slPctM[1]);
   115   else if (lossTickM) stop_loss_pct = Math.min(+(parseFloat(lossTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 20);
   116 
   117   if (tpPctM) take_profit_pct = parseFloat(tpPctM[1]);
   118   else if (profitTickM) take_profit_pct = Math.min(+(parseFloat(profitTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50);
   119 
   120   // position size input if any
   121   const posSizeM = code.match(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:position.?size|size|qty)[^"']*["']/i);
   122   const position_size_pct = posSizeM ? parseFloat(posSizeM[1]) : null;
   123 
   124   return { stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, position_size_pct };
   125 }
   126 
   127 function buildInterpretation(code: string, p: StrategyParams, risk: { stop_loss_pct: number | null; take_profit_pct: number | null; position_size_pct: number | null }): string {
   128   const lower = code.toLowerCase();
   129   const findings: string[] = [];
   130   if (lower.includes('rsi')) findings.push('• RSI — momentum oscillator');
   131   if (lower.includes('macd')) findings.push('• MACD — trend-following momentum');
   132   if (lower.includes('ema') || lower.includes('sma')) findings.push('• Moving Averages (EMA/SMA) — trend confirmation');
   133   if (lower.includes('bollinger') || lower.includes('bb.')) findings.push('• Bollinger Bands — volatility');
   134   if (lower.includes('stoch')) findings.push('• Stochastic — momentum');
   135   if (lower.includes('atr')) findings.push('• ATR — volatility/stop sizing');
   136   if (lower.includes('volume')) findings.push('• Volume — signal confirmation');
   137 
   138   const linesCount = code.split('\n').length;
   139   const v5 = code.includes('@version=5');
   140   const isStrat = lower.includes('strategy(');
   141 
   142   let r = `📊 AI Strategy Analysis\n\n`;
   143   r += `Type: ${isStrat ? 'Full Strategy' : 'Indicator'} | Version: PineScript ${v5 ? 'v5' : 'v4'} | Lines: ${linesCount}\n\n`;
   144   if (findings.length) r += `🔬 Indicators:\n${findings.join('\n')}\n\n`;
   145 
   146   r += `⚙️ Extracted Parameters:\n`;
   147   r += `• RSI Length: ${p.rsi_length} | Overbought: ${p.overbought} | Oversold: ${p.oversold}\n`;
   148   r += `• EMA Fast: ${p.ema_fast} | EMA Slow: ${p.ema_slow}\n`;
   149   r += `• Trade Direction: ${p.trade_direction} | Symbol: ${p.symbol}\n\n`;

```
/** Extract stop-loss and take-profit percentages from PineScript strategy.exit / input definitions */
function extractRiskPct(code: string): { stop_loss_pct: number | null; take_profit_pct: number | null; position_size_pct: number | null } {
  // strategy.exit("TP/SL", profit=200, loss=100)  → ticks, approximate as pct (1 tick ≈ 0.01%)
  const lossTickM = code.match(/loss\s*=\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i);
  const profitTickM = code.match(/profit\s*=\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i);

  // input.float(2.0, "Stop Loss %") or input(2, "SL")
  const slPctM = code.match(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:stop.?loss|sl|stop)[^"']*["']/i);
  const tpPctM = code.match(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:take.?profit|tp|target)[^"']*["']/i);

  let stop_loss_pct: number | null = null;
  let take_profit_pct: number | null = null;

  if (slPctM) stop_loss_pct = parseFloat(slPctM[1]);
  else if (lossTickM) stop_loss_pct = Math.min(+(parseFloat(lossTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 20);

  if (tpPctM) take_profit_pct = parseFloat(tpPctM[1]);
  else if (profitTickM) take_profit_pct = Math.min(+(parseFloat(profitTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50);

  // position size input if any
  const posSizeM = code.match(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:position.?size|size|qty)[^"']*["']/i);
  const position_size_pct = posSizeM ? parseFloat(posSizeM[1]) : null;

  return { stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, position_size_pct };
}
```
New String: ```
/** Extract stop-loss, single TP, and multi-TP (TP1/TP2/TP3) from PineScript */
function extractRiskPct(code: string): {
  stop_loss_pct: number | null;
  take_profit_pct: number | null;
  position_size_pct: number | null;
  tp1_pct: number | null; tp2_pct: number | null; tp3_pct: number | null;
  tp1_size_pct: number | null; tp2_size_pct: number | null; tp3_size_pct: number | null;
} {
  const flt = (pattern: RegExp) => {
    const m = code.match(pattern);
    return m ? parseFloat(m[1]) : null;
  };

  // ── Stop Loss ──
  const slInput = flt(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:stop.?loss|[^"']*\bsl\b)[^"']*["']/i);
  const lossTickM = code.match(/loss\s*=\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i);
  const stop_loss_pct = slInput ?? (lossTickM ? Math.min(+(parseFloat(lossTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 20) : null);

  // ── Position Size ──
  const position_size_pct = flt(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:position.?size|size|qty)[^"']*["']/i);

  // ── Multi-TP: input.float(1.5, "TP1 %") / input.float(3, "TP1") / tp1 = input.float(1.5, "Take Profit 1") ──
  const tp1Input = flt(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:tp1|tp\s*1|take.?profit\s*1|target\s*1)[^"']*["']/i);
  const tp2Input = flt(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:tp2|tp\s*2|take.?profit\s*2|target\s*2)[^"']*["']/i);
  const tp3Input = flt(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:tp3|tp\s*3|take.?profit\s*3|target\s*3)[^"']*["']/i);

  // ── Multi-TP: strategy.exit("TP1", ..., profit=150, qty_percent=33) ──
  const exitBlocks = [...code.matchAll(/strategy\.exit\s*\(\s*["']([^"']*?)["'][^)]*profit\s*=\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)[^)]*(?:qty_percent\s*=\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?))?/gi)];

  let tp1_exit: number | null = null, tp2_exit: number | null = null, tp3_exit: number | null = null;
  let tp1s_exit: number | null = null, tp2s_exit: number | null = null, tp3s_exit: number | null = null;

  for (const b of exitBlocks) {
    const label = b[1].toLowerCase();
    const pct = Math.min(+(parseFloat(b[2]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50);
    const sz = b[3] ? parseFloat(b[3]) : null;
    if (label.includes('tp1') || label.includes('tp 1') || label.includes('target1') || label.includes('1')) {
      if (!tp1_exit) { tp1_exit = pct; tp1s_exit = sz; }
    } else if (label.includes('tp2') || label.includes('tp 2') || label.includes('target2') || label.includes('2')) {
      if (!tp2_exit) { tp2_exit = pct; tp2s_exit = sz; }
    } else if (label.includes('tp3') || label.includes('tp 3') || label.includes('target3') || label.includes('3')) {
      if (!tp3_exit) { tp3_exit = pct; tp3s_exit = sz; }
    }
  }

  // Fallback: single profit= tick
  const profitTickM = code.match(/profit\s*=\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i);
  const singleTpInput = flt(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:take.?profit|tp|target)[^"']*["']/i);

  const tp1_pct = tp1Input ?? tp1_exit;
  const tp2_pct = tp2Input ?? tp2_exit;
  const tp3_pct = tp3Input ?? tp3_exit;
  const tp1_size_pct = tp1s_exit;
  const tp2_size_pct = tp2s_exit;
  const tp3_size_pct = tp3s_exit;

  // single TP fallback (for backward-compat field)
  const take_profit_pct = tp1_pct ?? singleTpInput ??
    (profitTickM && !exitBlocks.length ? Math.min(+(parseFloat(profitTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50) : null);

  return { stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, position_size_pct, tp1_pct, tp2_pct, tp3_pct, tp1_size_pct, tp2_size_pct, tp3_size_pct };
}
```

```
function buildInterpretation(code: string, p: StrategyParams, risk: { stop_loss_pct: number | null; take_profit_pct: number | null; position_size_pct: number | null }): string {
```

New String: ```
function buildInterpretation(code: string, p: StrategyParams, risk: {
  stop_loss_pct: number | null; take_profit_pct: number | null; position_size_pct: number | null;
  tp1_pct: number | null; tp2_pct: number | null; tp3_pct: number | null;
  tp1_size_pct: number | null; tp2_size_pct: number | null; tp3_size_pct: number | null;
}): string {
  const lower = code.toLowerCase();
  const findings: string[] = [];
  if (lower.includes('rsi')) findings.push('• RSI — momentum oscillator');
  if (lower.includes('macd')) findings.push('• MACD — trend-following momentum');
  if (lower.includes('ema') || lower.includes('sma')) findings.push('• Moving Averages (EMA/SMA) — trend confirmation');
  if (lower.includes('bollinger') || lower.includes('bb.')) findings.push('• Bollinger Bands — volatility');
  if (lower.includes('stoch')) findings.push('• Stochastic — momentum');
  if (lower.includes('atr')) findings.push('• ATR — volatility/stop sizing');
  if (lower.includes('volume')) findings.push('• Volume — signal confirmation');

  const linesCount = code.split('\n').length;
  const v5 = code.includes('@version=5');
  const isStrat = lower.includes('strategy(');

  let r = `📊 AI Strategy Analysis\n\n`;
  r += `Type: ${isStrat ? 'Full Strategy' : 'Indicator'} | Version: PineScript ${v5 ? 'v5' : 'v4'} | Lines: ${linesCount}\n\n`;
  if (findings.length) r += `🔬 Indicators:\n${findings.join('\n')}\n\n`;

  r += `⚙️ Extracted Parameters:\n`;
  r += `• RSI Length: ${p.rsi_length} | Overbought: ${p.overbought} | Oversold: ${p.oversold}\n`;
  r += `• EMA Fast: ${p.ema_fast} | EMA Slow: ${p.ema_slow}\n`;
  r += `• Trade Direction: ${p.trade_direction} | Symbol: ${p.symbol}\n\n`;

  r += `🟢 Entry Conditions:\n`;
  if (lower.includes('ta.crossover')) r += `• RSI crosses above oversold (${p.oversold})\n`;
  if (lower.includes('ema_fast') || p.ema_fast) r += `• EMA${p.ema_fast} > EMA${p.ema_slow} (uptrend filter)\n`;

  r += `\n⚙️ Risk Management:\n`;
  r += p.has_stop_loss ? `• Stop Loss defined ✓` : `• ⚠️ No stop loss detected`;
  if (risk.stop_loss_pct) r += ` (≈ ${risk.stop_loss_pct}%)`;
  r += '\n';

  // Multi-TP summary
  const hasMultiTp = risk.tp1_pct || risk.tp2_pct || risk.tp3_pct;
  if (hasMultiTp) {
    r += `• Multi-Target Take Profits detected:\n`;
    if (risk.tp1_pct) r += `  TP1: ${risk.tp1_pct}%${risk.tp1_size_pct ? ` (${risk.tp1_size_pct}% of position)` : ''}\n`;
    if (risk.tp2_pct) r += `  TP2: ${risk.tp2_pct}%${risk.tp2_size_pct ? ` (${risk.tp2_size_pct}% of position)` : ''}\n`;
    if (risk.tp3_pct) r += `  TP3: ${risk.tp3_pct}%${risk.tp3_size_pct ? ` (${risk.tp3_size_pct}% of position)` : ''}\n`;
  } else {
    r += p.has_take_profit ? `• Take Profit defined ✓` : `• ⚠️ No take profit detected`;
    if (risk.take_profit_pct) r += ` (≈ ${risk.take_profit_pct}%)`;
    r += '\n';
  }
  if (risk.position_size_pct) r += `• Position Size: ${risk.position_size_pct}% of balance\n`;

  r += `\n⚡ Bot Integration:\nWhen activated, the bot fetches live ${p.symbol} klines, computes RSI(${p.rsi_length}) and EMA${p.ema_fast}/EMA${p.ema_slow}, then places a ${p.trade_direction} order on Binance when entry conditions are met.`;
  return r;
}
```

New String: ```
  /* 6. Log trade to DB */
  if (order) {
    // Use TP1 as primary take_profit for DB record; log multi-TP as metadata in reason
    const tpLevels = [tp1, tp2, tp3].filter(Boolean);
    const multiTpNote = tpLevels.length > 1
      ? ` | TP levels: ${tpLevels.map((t, i) => `TP${i+1}=${t}%`).join(', ')}`
      : '';
    await client.from('trades').insert({
      user_id: userId,
      signal_id: null,
      symbol: params.symbol,
      direction: side === 'BUY' ? 'buy' : 'sell',
      entry_price: result.price,
      quantity: qty,
      stop_loss: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),
      take_profit: result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),
      status: 'open',
      binance_order_id: String(order.orderId ?? ''),
      opened_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    });

    /* 7. Log signal */
    await client.from('signals').insert({
      user_id: userId,
      strategy_id: body.strategyId,
      symbol: params.symbol,
      direction: side === 'BUY' ? 'buy' : 'sell',
      confidence: 85,
      entry_price: result.price,
      stop_loss: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),
      take_profit: result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),
      timeframe: params.timeframe,
      reason: result.reason + multiTpNote,
      status: 'executed',
    });
  }

  return json({
    signal: result.signal,
    reason: result.reason,
    rsi: result.rsi,
    ema_fast: result.ema_fast,
    ema_slow: result.ema_slow,

    quantity: qty,
    symbol: params.symbol,

    tp1: tp1 ? result.price * (1 + tp1 / 100) : result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),
```

```
                              onChange={e => setRiskForm(f => ({ ...f, [`${key}_pct`]: e.target.value }))}
                              className="h-7 bg-input border-border text-xs data-mono" />
                          </div>
                          <div className="space-y-0.5">
                            <Label className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">Close %</Label>
                            <Input type="number" min={1} max={100} step={1} placeholder={key === 'tp1' ? '33' : key === 'tp2' ? '33' : '34'}
                              value={riskForm[`${key}_size_pct`]}
                              onChange={e => setRiskForm(f => ({ ...f, [`${key}_size_pct`]: e.target.value }))}
                              className="h-7 bg-input border-border text-xs data-mono" />
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>

                    {/* AI extracted hint */}
                    {(selectedStrategy.tp1_pct || selectedStrategy.stop_loss_pct) && (
                      <p className="text-[10px] text-success flex items-center gap-1 flex-wrap">
                        ✓ AI extracted from PineScript —
                        {selectedStrategy.stop_loss_pct ? ` SL: ${selectedStrategy.stop_loss_pct}%` : ''}
                        {selectedStrategy.tp1_pct ? ` TP1: ${selectedStrategy.tp1_pct}%` : ''}
                        {selectedStrategy.tp2_pct ? ` TP2: ${selectedStrategy.tp2_pct}%` : ''}
                        {selectedStrategy.tp3_pct ? ` TP3: ${selectedStrategy.tp3_pct}%` : ''}
                        {selectedStrategy.position_size_pct ? ` Size: ${selectedStrategy.position_size_pct}%` : ''}
                      </p>
                    )}
                    <Button size="sm" onClick={handleSaveRisk} disabled={savingRisk} className="h-8 gap-1.5 w-full">
                      {savingRisk ? <Loader2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5 animate-spin" /> : <Save className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
                      Save Risk Settings
                    </Button>
                  </div>
```

ARGUMENTS: {'name': 'analyze-pinescript', 'appId': 'app-ckp4ck3tg3r5', 'userId': 'user-ckp2kzbr4m4g', 'appType': 'Web', 'files': [{'path': '/workspace/app-ckp4ck3tg3r5/supabase/functions/analyze-pinescript/index.ts', 'name': 'index.ts', 'content': 'import { createClient } from \'jsr:@supabase/supabase-js@2\';\n\nconst corsHeaders = {\n  \'Access-Control-Allow-Origin\': \'*\',\n  \'Access-Control-Allow-Headers\': \'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type\',\n};\n\ninterface StrategyParams {\n  rsi_length: number;\n  overbought: number;\n  oversold: number;\n  ema_fast: number;\n  ema_slow: number;\n  symbol: string;\n  timeframe: string;\n  has_stop_loss: boolean;\n  has_take_profit: boolean;\n  trade_direction: \'long\' | \'short\' | \'both\';\n}\n\nDeno.serve(async (req) => {\n  if (req.method === \'OPTIONS\') return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });\n\n  try {\n    const { strategyId, code } = await req.json();\n\n    if (!code) {\n      return new Response(\n        JSON.stringify({ error: \'PineScript code is required\' }),\n        { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' } }\n      );\n    }\n\n    const params = extractParams(code);\n    const risk = extractRiskPct(code);\n    const interpretation = buildInterpretation(code, params, risk);\n\n    if (strategyId) {\n      const supabase = createClient(\n        Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_URL\') ?? \'\',\n        Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY\') ?? \'\'\n      );\n      const update: Record<string, unknown> = { ai_interpretation: interpretation, strategy_params: params };\n      if (risk.stop_loss_pct !== null) update.stop_loss_pct = risk.stop_loss_pct;\n      if (risk.take_profit_pct !== null) update.take_profit_pct = risk.take_profit_pct;\n      if (risk.position_size_pct !== null) update.position_size_pct = risk.position_size_pct;\n      if (risk.tp1_pct !== null) update.tp1_pct = risk.tp1_pct;\n      if (risk.tp2_pct !== null) update.tp2_pct = risk.tp2_pct;\n      if (risk.tp3_pct !== null) update.tp3_pct = risk.tp3_pct;\n      if (risk.tp1_size_pct !== null) update.tp1_size_pct = risk.tp1_size_pct;\n      if (risk.tp2_size_pct !== null) update.tp2_size_pct = risk.tp2_size_pct;\n      if (risk.tp3_size_pct !== null) update.tp3_size_pct = risk.tp3_size_pct;\n      await supabase.from(\'strategies\').update(update).eq(\'id\', strategyId);\n    }\n\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ interpretation, params, risk }),\n      { headers: { ...corsHeaders, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' } }\n    );\n  } catch (err) {\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : \'Analysis failed\' }),\n      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' } }\n    );\n  }\n});\n\n/** Extract numeric parameters from PineScript using regex patterns */\nfunction extractParams(code: string): StrategyParams {\n  const num = (pattern: RegExp, fallback: number) => {\n    const m = code.match(pattern);\n    return m ? parseInt(m[1], 10) : fallback;\n  };\n\n  const rsi_length = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?RSI/i, 0) ||\n    num(/ta\\.rsi\\s*\\(\\s*\\w+\\s*,\\s*(\\d+)\\s*\\)/i, 14);\n\n  const overbought = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?overbought/i, 0) ||\n    num(/overbought\\s*=\\s*(\\d+)/i, 70);\n\n  const oversold = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?oversold/i, 0) ||\n    num(/oversold\\s*=\\s*(\\d+)/i, 30);\n\n  const emaMatches = [...code.matchAll(/ta\\.ema\\s*\\(\\s*\\w+\\s*,\\s*(\\d+)\\s*\\)/gi)]\n    .map(m => parseInt(m[1], 10))\n    .sort((a, b) => a - b);\n\n  const ema_fast = emaMatches[0] ?? num(/ema_fast\\s*=.*?(\\d+)/i, 20);\n  const ema_slow = emaMatches[1] ?? num(/ema_slow\\s*=.*?(\\d+)/i, 50);\n\n  const symbolHint = code.match(/\\b(BTCUSDT|ETHUSDT|SOLUSDT|BNBUSDT)\\b/i);\n  const symbol = symbolHint ? symbolHint[1].toUpperCase() : \'BTCUSDT\';\n\n  const tfMatch = code.match(/timeframe\\s*[=:]\\s*["\']([^"\']+)["\']/i);\n  const timeframe = tfMatch ? tfMatch[1] : \'1h\';\n\n  const lower = code.toLowerCase();\n  const has_stop_loss = lower.includes(\'loss=\') || lower.includes(\'stop_loss\') || lower.includes(\'strategy.exit\');\n  const has_take_profit = lower.includes(\'profit=\') || lower.includes(\'take_profit\');\n  const hasLong = lower.includes(\'strategy.long\');\n  const hasShort = lower.includes(\'strategy.short\');\n  const trade_direction: \'long\' | \'short\' | \'both\' = (hasLong && hasShort) ? \'both\' : hasShort ? \'short\' : \'long\';\n\n  return { rsi_length, overbought, oversold, ema_fast, ema_slow, symbol, timeframe, has_stop_loss, has_take_profit, trade_direction };\n}\n\n/** Extract stop-loss, single TP, and multi-TP (TP1/TP2/TP3) from PineScript */\nfunction extractRiskPct(code: string): {\n  stop_loss_pct: number | null;\n  take_profit_pct: number | null;\n  position_size_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_pct: number | null; tp2_pct: number | null; tp3_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_size_pct: number | null; tp2_size_pct: number | null; tp3_size_pct: number | null;\n} {\n  const flt = (pattern: RegExp) => {\n    const m = code.match(pattern);\n    return m ? parseFloat(m[1]) : null;\n  };\n\n  // ── Stop Loss ──\n  const slInput = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:stop.?loss|[^"\']*\\bsl\\b)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n  const lossTickM = code.match(/loss\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)/i);\n  const stop_loss_pct = slInput ?? (lossTickM ? Math.min(+(parseFloat(lossTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 20) : null);\n\n  // ── Position Size ──\n  const position_size_pct = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:position.?size|size|qty)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n\n  // ── Multi-TP: input.float(1.5, "TP1 %") / input.float(3, "TP1") / tp1 = input.float(1.5, "Take Profit 1") ──\n  const tp1Input = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:tp1|tp\\s*1|take.?profit\\s*1|target\\s*1)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n  const tp2Input = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:tp2|tp\\s*2|take.?profit\\s*2|target\\s*2)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n  const tp3Input = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:tp3|tp\\s*3|take.?profit\\s*3|target\\s*3)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n\n  // ── Multi-TP: strategy.exit("TP1", ..., profit=150, qty_percent=33) ──\n  const exitBlocks = [...code.matchAll(/strategy\\.exit\\s*\\(\\s*["\']([^"\']*?)["\'][^)]*profit\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)[^)]*(?:qty_percent\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?))?/gi)];\n\n  let tp1_exit: number | null = null, tp2_exit: number | null = null, tp3_exit: number | null = null;\n  let tp1s_exit: number | null = null, tp2s_exit: number | null = null, tp3s_exit: number | null = null;\n\n  for (const b of exitBlocks) {\n    const label = b[1].toLowerCase();\n    const pct = Math.min(+(parseFloat(b[2]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50);\n    const sz = b[3] ? parseFloat(b[3]) : null;\n    if (label.includes(\'tp1\') || label.includes(\'tp 1\') || label.includes(\'target1\') || label.includes(\'1\')) {\n      if (!tp1_exit) { tp1_exit = pct; tp1s_exit = sz; }\n    } else if (label.includes(\'tp2\') || label.includes(\'tp 2\') || label.includes(\'target2\') || label.includes(\'2\')) {\n      if (!tp2_exit) { tp2_exit = pct; tp2s_exit = sz; }\n    } else if (label.includes(\'tp3\') || label.includes(\'tp 3\') || label.includes(\'target3\') || label.includes(\'3\')) {\n      if (!tp3_exit) { tp3_exit = pct; tp3s_exit = sz; }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Fallback: single profit= tick\n  const profitTickM = code.match(/profit\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)/i);\n  const singleTpInput = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:take.?profit|tp|target)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n\n  const tp1_pct = tp1Input ?? tp1_exit;\n  const tp2_pct = tp2Input ?? tp2_exit;\n  const tp3_pct = tp3Input ?? tp3_exit;\n  const tp1_size_pct = tp1s_exit;\n  const tp2_size_pct = tp2s_exit;\n  const tp3_size_pct = tp3s_exit;\n\n  // single TP fallback (for backward-compat field)\n  const take_profit_pct = tp1_pct ?? singleTpInput ??\n    (profitTickM && !exitBlocks.length ? Math.min(+(parseFloat(profitTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50) : null);\n\n  return { stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, position_size_pct, tp1_pct, tp2_pct, tp3_pct, tp1_size_pct, tp2_size_pct, tp3_size_pct };\n}\n\nfunction buildInterpretation(code: string, p: StrategyParams, risk: {\n  stop_loss_pct: number | null; take_profit_pct: number | null; position_size_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_pct: number | null; tp2_pct: number | null; tp3_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_size_pct: number | null; tp2_size_pct: number | null; tp3_size_pct: number | null;\n}): string {\n  const lower = code.toLowerCase();\n  const findings: string[] = [];\n  if (lower.includes(\'rsi\')) findings.push(\'• RSI — momentum oscillator\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'macd\')) findings.push(\'• MACD — trend-following momentum\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'ema\') || lower.includes(\'sma\')) findings.push(\'• Moving Averages (EMA/SMA) — trend confirmation\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'bollinger\') || lower.includes(\'bb.\')) findings.push(\'• Bollinger Bands — volatility\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'stoch\')) findings.push(\'• Stochastic — momentum\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'atr\')) findings.push(\'• ATR — volatility/stop sizing\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'volume\')) findings.push(\'• Volume — signal confirmation\');\n\n  const linesCount = code.split(\'\\n\').length;\n  const v5 = code.includes(\'@version=5\');\n  const isStrat = lower.includes(\'strategy(\');\n\n  let r = `📊 AI Strategy Analysis\\n\\n`;\n  r += `Type: ${isStrat ? \'Full Strategy\' : \'Indicator\'} | Version: PineScript ${v5 ? \'v5\' : \'v4\'} | Lines: ${linesCount}\\n\\n`;\n  if (findings.length) r += `🔬 Indicators:\\n${findings.join(\'\\n\')}\\n\\n`;\n\n  r += `⚙️ Extracted Parameters:\\n`;\n  r += `• RSI Length: ${p.rsi_length} | Overbought: ${p.overbought} | Oversold: ${p.oversold}\\n`;\n  r += `• EMA Fast: ${p.ema_fast} | EMA Slow: ${p.ema_slow}\\n`;\n  r += `• Trade Direction: ${p.trade_direction} | Symbol: ${p.symbol}\\n\\n`;\n\n  r += `🟢 Entry Conditions:\\n`;\n  if (lower.includes(\'ta.crossover\')) r += `• RSI crosses above oversold (${p.oversold})\\n`;\n  if (lower.includes(\'ema_fast\') || p.ema_fast) r += `• EMA${p.ema_fast} > EMA${p.ema_slow} (uptrend filter)\\n`;\n\n  r += `\\n⚙️ Risk Management:\\n`;\n  r += p.has_stop_loss ? `• Stop Loss defined ✓` : `• ⚠️ No stop loss detected`;\n  if (risk.stop_loss_pct) r += ` (≈ ${risk.stop_loss_pct}%)`;\n  r += \'\\n\';\n\n  // Multi-TP summary\n  const hasMultiTp = risk.tp1_pct || risk.tp2_pct || risk.tp3_pct;\n  if (hasMultiTp) {\n    r += `• Multi-Target Take Profits detected:\\n`;\n    if (risk.tp1_pct) r += `  TP1: ${risk.tp1_pct}%${risk.tp1_size_pct ? ` (${risk.tp1_size_pct}% of position)` : \'\'}\\n`;\n    if (risk.tp2_pct) r += `  TP2: ${risk.tp2_pct}%${risk.tp2_size_pct ? ` (${risk.tp2_size_pct}% of position)` : \'\'}\\n`;\n    if (risk.tp3_pct) r += `  TP3: ${risk.tp3_pct}%${risk.tp3_size_pct ? ` (${risk.tp3_size_pct}% of position)` : \'\'}\\n`;\n  } else {\n    r += p.has_take_profit ? `• Take Profit defined ✓` : `• ⚠️ No take profit detected`;\n    if (risk.take_profit_pct) r += ` (≈ ${risk.take_profit_pct}%)`;\n    r += \'\\n\';\n  }\n  if (risk.position_size_pct) r += `• Position Size: ${risk.position_size_pct}% of balance\\n`;\n\n  r += `\\n⚡ Bot Integration:\\nWhen activated, the bot fetches live ${p.symbol} klines, computes RSI(${p.rsi_length}) and EMA${p.ema_fast}/EMA${p.ema_slow}, then places a ${p.trade_direction} order on Binance when entry conditions are met.`;\n  return r;\n}\n'}]}

overbought: number;\n  oversold: number;\n  ema_fast: number;\n  ema_slow: number;\n  symbol: string;\n  timeframe: string;\n  has_stop_loss: boolean;\n  has_take_profit: boolean;\n  trade_direction: gains = 0, losses = 0;\n  for (let i = closes.length - period; i < closes.length; i++) {\n    const diff = closes[i] - closes[i - 1];\n    if (diff > 0) gains += diff; else losses -= diff;\n  }\n  const avgGain = gains / period;\n  const avgLoss = losses / period;\n  if (avgLoss === 0) return 100;\n  const rs = avgGain / avgLoss;\n  return +(100 - 100 / (1 + rs)).toFixed(2);\n}\n\nfunction calcEMA(closes: number[], period: number): number {\n  if (closes.length < period) return closes[closes.length - 1];\n  const k = 2 / (period + 1);\n  let ema = closes.slice(0, period).reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / period;\n  for (let i = period; i < closes.length; i++) {\n    ema = closes[i] * k + ema * (1 - k);\n  }\n  return +ema.toFixed(6);\n}\n\n/* ─── Signal evaluation ─── */\nfunction evaluateSignal(closes: number[], params: StrategyParams): SignalResult {\n  const rsi = calcRSI(closes, params.rsi_length);\n  const emaF = calcEMA(closes, params.ema_fast);\n  const emaS = params.trade_direction === \'long\' || params.trade_direction === \'both\';\n  const canShort = params.trade_direction === \'short\' || params.trade_direction === \'both\';\n\n  if (canLong && EMA${params.ema_fast}=${emaF.toFixed(2)} | EMA${params.ema_slow}=${emaS.toFixed(2)} — no entry condition met`,\n    rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price,\n  };\n}\n\n/* ─── Minimum notional \'https://api.binance.com\';\nconst BINANCE_BASE_TEST = \'https://testnet.binance.vision\';\nconst RECV_WINDOW = \'5000\';\n\n/* ─── Types ─── */\ninterface StrategyParams {\n  rsi_length: number;\n  overbought: number;\n  oversold: number;\n  ema_fast: number;\n  ema_slow: number;\n  symbol: string;\n  timeframe: string;\n  has_stop_loss: boolean;\n  has_take_profit: boolean;\n  trade_direction: \'long\' | \'short\' | \'both\';\n}\n\ninterface OHLCV {\n  close: number;\n  high: number;\n  low: number;\n}\n\ninterface SignalResult {\n  signal: \'BUY\' | \'SELL\' | \'HOLD\';\n  reason: string;\n  rsi: number;\n  ema_fast: number;\n  ema_slow: number;\n  price: number;\n}\n\n/* ─── Supabase service client ─── */\nfunction sb() {\n  return createClient(\n    Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_URL\')!,\n    Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY\')!,\n  );\n}\n\n/* ─── Binance helpers ─── */\nasync function hmacSha256(secret: string, msg: string): Promise<string> {\n  const enc = new TextEncoder();\n  const key = await crypto.subtle.importKey(\'raw\', enc.encode(secret), { name: \'HMAC\', hash: \'SHA-256\' }, false, [\'sign\']);\n  const sig = await crypto.subtle.sign(\'HMAC\', key, enc.encode(msg));\n  return Array.from(new Uint8Array(sig)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, \'0\')).join(\'\');\n}\n\nasync function signedPost(base: string, path: string, apiKey: string, secret: string, params: Record<string, string>) {\n  const ts = Date.now().toString();\n  const all = { ...params, recvWindow: RECV_WINDOW, timestamp: ts };\n  const qs = new URLSearchParams(all).toString();\n  const sig = await hmacSha256(secret, qs);\n  const res = await fetch(`${base}${path}?${qs}&signature=${sig}`, {\n    method: \'POST\',\n    headers: { \'X-MBX-APIKEY\': apiKey, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n  });\n  const json = await res.json();\n  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(json.msg || `HTTP ${res.status}`);\n  return json;\n}\n\nasync function fetchKlines(base: string, symbol: string, interval: string, limit: number): Promise<OHLCV[]> {\n  const url = `${base}/api/v3/klines?symbol=${symbol.toUpperCase()}&interval=${interval}&limit=${limit}`;\n  const res = await fetch(url, { signal: AbortSignal.timeout(10_000) });\n  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Klines fetch failed: ${res.status}`);\n  const raw: unknown[][] = await res.json();\n  return raw.map(c => ({\n    close: parseFloat(c[4] as string),\n    high: parseFloat(c[2] as string),\n    low: parseFloat(c[3] as string),\n  }));\n}\n\n/* ─── Technical Indicators ─── */\nfunction calcRSI(closes: number[], period: number): number {\n  if (closes.length < period + 1) return 50;\n  let gains = 0, losses = 0;\n  for (let i = closes.length - period; i < closes.length; i++) {\n    const diff = closes[i] - closes[i - 1];\n    if (diff > 0) gains += diff; else losses -= diff;\n  }\n  const avgGain = gains / period;\n  const avgLoss = losses / period;\n  if (avgLoss === 0) return 100;\n  const rs = avgGain / avgLoss;\n  return +(100 - 100 / (1 + rs)).toFixed(2);\n}\n\nfunction calcEMA(closes: number[], period: number): number {\n  if (closes.length < period) return closes[closes.length - 1];\n  const k = 2 / (period + 1);\n  let ema = closes.slice(0, period).reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / period;\n  for (let i = period; i < closes.length; i++) {\n    ema = closes[i] * k + ema * (1 - k);\n  }\n  return +ema.toFixed(6);\n}\n\n/* ─── Signal evaluation ─── */\nfunction evaluateSignal(closes: number[], params: StrategyParams): SignalResult {\n  const rsi = calcRSI(closes, params.rsi_length);\n  const emaF = calcEMA(closes, params.ema_fast);\n  const emaS = calcEMA(closes, params.ema_slow);\n  const price = closes[closes.length - 1];\n\n  const prevRsi = calcRSI(closes.slice(0, -1), params.rsi_length);\n  const bullishCross = prevRsi <= params.oversold && rsi > params.oversold;\n  const bearishCross = prevRsi >= params.overbought && rsi < params.overbought;\n  const uptrend = emaF > emaS;\n  const downtrend = emaF < emaS;\n\n  const canLong = params.trade_direction === \'long\' || params.trade_direction === \'both\';\n  const canShort = params.trade_direction === \'short\' || params.trade_direction === \'both\';\n\n  if (canLong && bullishCross && uptrend) {\n    return { signal: \'BUY\', reason: `RSI crossed above oversold (${params.oversold}) with EMA${params.ema_fast} > EMA${params.ema_slow} uptrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price };\n  }\n  if (canShort && bearishCross && downtrend) {\n    return { signal: \'SELL\', reason: `RSI crossed below overbought (${params.overbought}) with EMA${params.ema_fast} < EMA${params.ema_slow} downtrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price };\n  }\n\n  return {\n    signal: \'HOLD\',\n    reason: `RSI=${rsi} | EMA${params.ema_fast}=${emaF.toFixed(2)} | EMA${params.ema_slow}=${emaS.toFixed(2)} — no entry condition met`,\n    rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price,\n  };\n}\n\n/* ─── Minimum notional helper (USDT pairs) ─── */\nfunction calcQuantity(price: number, positionPct: number, _symbol: string): number {\n  const budget = 1000 * (positionPct / 100); // assume $1000 base (real: fetch account balance)\n  const qty = budget / price;\n  // round to reasonable precision\n  if (price > 1000) return +qty.toFixed(5);\n  if (price > 1) return +qty.toFixed(3);\n  return +qty.toFixed(1);\n}\n\nconst TF_INTERVAL: Record<string, string> = {\n  \'1m\': \'1m\', \'5m\': \'5m\', \'15m\': \'15m\', \'30m\': \'30m\',\n  \'1h\': \'1h\', \'4h\': \'4h\', \'1d\': \'1d\',\n};\n\n/* ─── Main handler ─── */\nDeno.serve(async (req) => {\n  if (req.method === \'OPTIONS\') return new Response(\'ok\', { headers: corsHeaders });\n\n  const authHeader = req.headers.get(\'authorization\') || \'\';\n  const token = authHeader.replace(\'Bearer \', \'\');\n  if (!token) return json({ error: \'Missing authorization\' }, 401);\n\n  let userId = \'\';\n  try {\n    const payload = JSON.parse(atob(token.split(\'.\')[1]));\n    userId = payload.sub;\n  } catch {\n    return json({ error: \'Invalid token\' }, 401);\n  }\n\n  let body: { strategyId: string };\n  try { body = await req.json(); } catch { return json({ error: \'Invalid JSON\' }, 400); }\n  if (!body.strategyId) return json({ error: \'strategyId is required\' }, 400);\n\n  const client = sb();\n\n  /* 1. Load strategy */\n  const { data: strategy, error: stratErr } = await client\n    .from(\'strategies\')\n    .select(\'*\')\n    .eq(\'id\', body.strategyId)\n    .eq(\'user_id\', userId)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  if (stratErr || !strategy) return json({ error: \'Strategy not found\' }, 404);\n\n  const params = strategy.strategy_params as StrategyParams | null;\n  if (!params) return json({ error: \'Strategy not analyzed yet. Click "AI Analyze" first.\' }, 400);\n\n  /* 2. Load user settings (API keys + risk params + testnet flag) */\n  const { data: settings } = await client\n    .from(\'user_settings\')\n    .select(\'binance_api_key, binance_api_secret, use_testnet, bot_enabled, position_size_pct, stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, min_confidence\')\n    .eq(\'user_id\', userId)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  if (!settings?.binance_api_key || !settings?.binance_api_secret) {\n    return json({ error: \'Binance API keys not configured in Settings.\' }, 400);\n  }\n\n  const useTestnet: boolean = settings.use_testnet ?? true;\n  const base = useTestnet ? BINANCE_BASE_TEST : BINANCE_BASE_REAL;\n\n  // Priority: per-strategy values > global user_settings fallback\n  const effectiveSL: number = (strategy.stop_loss_pct ?? settings.stop_loss_pct ?? 2);\n  const effectiveTP: number = (strategy.tp1_pct ?? strategy.take_profit_pct ?? settings.take_profit_pct ?? 4);\n  const effectiveSize: number = (strategy.position_size_pct ?? settings.position_size_pct ?? 5);\n  // Multi-TP levels (null = not configured)\n  const tp1: number | null = strategy.tp1_pct ?? null;\n  const tp2: number | null = strategy.tp2_pct ?? null;\n  const tp3: number | null = strategy.tp3_pct ?? null;\n  const tp1Size: number = strategy.tp1_size_pct ?? 33;\n  const tp2Size: number = strategy.tp2_size_pct ?? 33;\n  const tp3Size: number = strategy.tp3_size_pct ?? 34;\n\n  /* 3. Fetch live klines */\n  const interval = TF_INTERVAL[params.timeframe] ?? \'1h\';\n  const klineLimit = Math.max(params.rsi_length + 10, params.ema_slow + 10, 60);\n  let candles: OHLCV[];\n  try {\n    candles = await fetchKlines(base, params.symbol, interval, klineLimit);\n  } catch (e: unknown) {\n    return json({ error: `Binance klines error: ${(e as Error).message}` }, 502);\n  }\n\n  const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);\n\n  /* 4. Evaluate signal */\n  const result = evaluateSignal(closes, params);\n\n  if (result.signal === \'HOLD\') {\n    return json({ signal: \'HOLD\', ...result, mode: useTestnet ? \'testnet\' : \'real\', symbol: params.symbol });\n  }\n\n  /* 5. Place order */\n  const side = result.signal; // \'BUY\' | \'SELL\'\n  const qty = calcQuantity(result.price, effectiveSize, params.symbol);\n\n  let order: Record<string, unknown> | null = null;\n  let orderError: string | null = null;\n  try {\n    order = await signedPost(base, \'/api/v3/order\', settings.binance_api_key, settings.binance_api_secret, {\n      symbol: params.symbol.toUpperCase(),\n      side,\n      type: \'MARKET\',\n      quantity: String(qty),\n    });\n  } catch (e: unknown) {\n    orderError = (e as Error).message;\n  }\n\n  /* 6. Log trade to DB */\n  if (order) {\n    // Use TP1 as primary take_profit for DB record; log multi-TP as metadata in reason\n    const tpLevels = [tp1, tp2, tp3].filter(Boolean);\n    const multiTpNote = tpLevels.length > 1\n      ? ` | TP levels: ${tpLevels.map((t, i) => `TP${i+1}=${t}%`).join(\', \')}`\n      : \'\';\n    await client.from(\'trades\').insert({\n      user_id: userId,\n      signal_id: null,\n      symbol: params.symbol,\n      direction: side === \'BUY\' ? \'buy\' : \'sell\',\n      entry_price: result.price,\n      quantity: qty,\n      stop_loss: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),\n      take_profit: result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),\n      status: \'open\',\n      binance_order_id: String(order.orderId ?? \'\'),\n      opened_at: new Date().toISOString(),\n    });\n\n    /* 7. Log signal */\n    await client.from(\'signals\').insert({\n      user_id: userId,\n      strategy_id: body.strategyId,\n      symbol: params.symbol,\n      direction: side === \'BUY\' ? \'buy\' : \'sell\',\n      confidence: 85,\n      entry_price: result.price,\n      stop_loss: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),\n      take_profit: result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),\n      timeframe: params.timeframe,\n      reason: result.reason + multiTpNote,\n      status: \'executed\',\n    });\n  }\n\n  return json({\n    signal: result.signal,\n    reason: result.reason,\n    rsi: result.rsi,\n    ema_fast: result.ema_fast,\n    ema_slow: result.ema_slow,\n    price: result.price,\n    quantity: qty,\n    symbol: params.symbol,\n    sl: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),\n    tp1: tp1 ? result.price * (1 + tp1 / 100) : result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),\n    tp2: tp2 ? result.price * (1 + tp2 / 100) : null,\n    tp3: tp3 ? result.price * (1 + tp3 / 100) : null,\n    tp1Size, tp2Size, tp3Size,\n    mode: useTestnet ? \'testnet\' : \'real\',\n    order: order ?? null,\n    orderError,\n  });\n});\n\nfunction json(data: unknown, status = 200) {\n  return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {\n    status,\n    headers: { ...corsHeaders, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n  });\n}\n'}]}

New String:
```
  const runAnalyze = async (strategy: Strategy, showToast = true) => {
    setInterpreting(strategy.id);
    const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('analyze-pinescript', {
      body: { strategyId: strategy.id, code: strategy.pinescript_code },
      method: 'POST',
    });
    if (error || !data?.interpretation) {
      const fallback = `📊 Strategy Analysis: "${strategy.name}"\n\n` +
        `• Entry signals detected in PineScript code\n` +
        `• Uses RSI momentum indicators\n` +
        `• Trend confirmation via EMA crossovers\n` +
        `• Risk management: stop loss and take profit defined\n\n` +
        `⚡ Bot will monitor for entry conditions matching this strategy and execute trades via your Binance API.`;
      await updateStrategy(strategy.id, { ai_interpretation: fallback });
      if (showToast) toast.success('Strategy analyzed (demo mode)');
    } else {
```
```
      if (showToast) {
        const risk = data.risk as { tp1_pct?: number; tp2_pct?: number; tp3_pct?: number; stop_loss_pct?: number } | undefined;
        const extracted: string[] = [];
        if (risk?.stop_loss_pct) extracted.push(`SL: ${risk.stop_loss_pct}%`);
        if (risk?.tp1_pct) extracted.push(`TP1: ${risk.tp1_pct}%`);
        if (risk?.tp2_pct) extracted.push(`TP2: ${risk.tp2_pct}%`);
        if (risk?.tp3_pct) extracted.push(`TP3: ${risk.tp3_pct}%`);
        const hint = extracted.length ? ` — Extracted: ${extracted.join(', ')}` : '';
        toast.success(`Strategy analyzed by AI!${hint}`, { icon: '🤖', duration: 6000 });
      }
    }
    // Reload and auto-sync Risk Settings panel with extracted values
    const updated = await getStrategies();
    setStrategies(updated);
    const fresh = updated.find(s => s.id === strategy.id) ?? null;
    if (fresh) {
      // Always re-sync the panel — whether this is the selected strategy or auto-analyze on create
      if (selectedStrategy?.id === strategy.id || !showToast) {
        handleSelectStrategy(fresh);
      }
    }
    setInterpreting(null);
  };
```
